boing

Thanks for the update. However, due to the economic downturn, the payments will be made at a rate of one Canadian One Cent Piece (1 **¢** CAN) per annum. This method of payment will be continued until the end of life of the original claimant. Discounts for change of currency and conversion rates will be paid for in advance by the claimant. This credit will be used in lieu of payment until said credit is exhausted upon which time the debtor will begin said payment. The postage and all charges for the check, ink, paper, letter, etc. for posting the check must be paid to the debtor before payment shall be made.

### Post by jenkinbr on 2009-06-02
**[size=5][COLOR="DarkRed"][HowTo] Boing [[COLOR="DarkRed"]The Boing Thread[/COLOR]]("http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=999864") in 4 Easy Steps[/COLOR][/size]**
[list=1]
[*]While in [The Boing Thread]("http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=999864"), click on any Quick-Reply icon ([IMG]http://ubuntuforums.org/images/buttons/quickreply.gif[/IMG]) found in the lower right of any post on this thread.
[*]Type in the following:```
Boing
```
[*]Press the <tab> key, followed by the <enter> key.
[*]Repeat, taking care not to boing too quickly (be sure to wait 20 seconds and giving other boingers a chance to boing) and changing the text of your boing if you are boinging within five minutes of the previous boing.  This step is neccesary to keep Stupid Forum from barking errors at you, such as > **"Stupid Forum"]1. This forum requires that you wait 20 seconds between posts. Please try again in 1 second.[/quote] and [quote="Stupid Forum"]1. This post is a duplicate of a post that you have posted in the last 5 minutes.[/quote][/list]

Happy Boinging!

Don't believe me?  Try it!  But, under all circumstances, do play nice:

[QUOTE=Rocket2DMn said:**
> Being the top [s]bumper[/s] **boinger** won't do you any good when you get banned for spamming (and don't think I won't back that decision if it comes to it).  Play nice, please.

[s]*BUMP!*[/s]

***BOING!***

BOING

[size=1](This tutorial is a modified version of my [[HowTo] Bump The BUMP Thread]("http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?p=6306563#post6306563") Tutorial.)[/size]

### Post by Midnight Star on 2010-03-13
<tag = "boing">
     ; Boing version 1.0
     DO "Boing",640,400,infinite;
     WHILE WAIT "Boing"
          OUTPUT "Boing";
     IF NOT "Boing"
        THEN "Boing";
     RETURN
</tag>

### Post by nothingspecial on 2011-10-12
```
sudo apt-get install toilet
```

```
clear;toilet -S --gay boing; toilet --gay -S -F flip boing; toilet --gay -S -F flop boing; toilet -S --gay boing
```

:-\"

---

### Post by ubupirate on 2011-10-12
> **nothingspecial said:**
> ```
sudo apt-get install toilet
``````
clear;toilet -S --gay boing; toilet --gay -S -F flip boing; toilet --gay -S -F flop boing; toilet -S --gay boing
```:-\"

What's with the really unnecessary use of "gay" in there?


Boing.

---

### Post by nothingspecial on 2011-10-12
It's a command flag.

I'll remove it if you (or anyone else) find(s) it offensive.

It means print the output in bright, fancy colours, the original meaning of gay.

You can use metal if you like,
```

clear; f=100; while [[ f -ge 1 ]]; do toilet -S --metal boing; toilet --metal -S -F flip boing; toilet --metal -S -F flop boing; toilet -S --metal boing; f=$(( f - 1 )); done
```


(Press Ctrl-C to stop it although it will eventually)

### Post by kazztan0325 on 2012-04-24
&#12499;&#12520;&#12540;&#12531; [ biy&#333;n ]

( A Japanese onomatopoeia. It means the sound made by a elastic object (such as a spring) when bouncing; the sound of a bounce. That is to say, "&#12499;&#12520;&#12540;&#12531;!" = "**boing!**")
